**@MuRongPIG**
usage: .m <command> [arg1] [arg2] ...
|command|argument(s)|description|
|--|--|--|
|add|tripcode|adds tripcode to the operator list|
|remove|tripcode|removes tripcode from the operator list|
|listops||lists all operators|
|kick|nickname|kicks an user from the channel (can be whispered without '.m')|
|lockroom||prevents un-authed users from joining the channel|
|unlockroom||allows all users to join the channel|
|enablecap||enables captcha for the channel|
|disablecap||disables captcha for the channel|
Report any bugs to @AnnikaV9
